**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# LibreOffice Calc Formula Evaluation Chain

## Your Task

An on-call developer is investigating incorrect formula evaluation in LibreOffice Calc. Trace how a cell formula like `=SUM(A1:A10)` is parsed and evaluated. Find the key C++ source files in `LibreOffice/core` under `sc/` that implement the formula engine: 1. The file that implements the formula tokenizer/compiler (`sc/source/core/tool/compiler.cxx` or similar). 2. The file that implements `ScInterpreter` — the formula bytecode interpreter that evaluates formulas. 3. The file that defines `ScFormulaCell` — the cell type that holds a formula and its result. 4. The file that implements `ScRecalcMode` or recalculation scheduling — how Calc determines which cells need recalculation. Report each file path and key class/function.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the incident domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/libreoffice-core--9c8b85f3` (LibreOffice/core)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

1. **Formula Compiler/Tokenizer**
   - **`sc/inc/compiler.hxx`** - Header defining `ScCompiler` class
   - **`sc/source/core/tool/compiler.cxx`** - Implementation
   - The `ScCompiler` class parses formula strings into bytecode tokens

2. **Formula Interpreter** 
   - **`sc/source/core/inc/interpre.hxx`** - Header defining `ScInterpreter` class
   - **`sc/source/core/tool/interpr1.cxx` through `interpr8.cxx`** - Implementation split across 8 files
   - The `ScInterpreter` class executes compiled formulas using a stack-based bytecode interpreter

3. **Formula Cell**
   - **`sc/inc/formulacell.hxx`** - Header defining `ScFormulaCell` class
   - **`sc/source/core/data/formulacell.cxx`** - Implementation
   - The `ScFormulaCell` class represents cells containing formulas and coordinates interpretation

4. **Recalculation Scheduling**
   - **`include/formula/tokenarray.hxx`** - Defines `ScRecalcMode` enum (lines 59-69)
   - Enum values: `ALWAYS`, `ONLOAD_MUST`, `ONLOAD_ONCE`, `ONLOAD_LENIENT`, `NORMAL`, `FORCED`, `ONREFMOVE`
   - Controls when cells are marked for recalculation

## Evaluation Chain Flow

When a formula like `=SUM(A1:A10)` is entered:
1. **Parse** → `ScCompiler` tokenizes into bytecode
2. **Store** → `ScFormulaCell` holds tokens and recalc mode
3. **Execute** → `ScInterpreter` walks token array and produces result
4. **Broadcast** → Result notifications trigger dependent cell recalculations

The complete analysis has been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed references to class definitions, key methods, and the complete evaluation pipeline.

Formula Tokenizer/Compiler\\n\\n**Header File**: `sc/inc/compiler.hxx`\\n**Implementation File**: `sc/source/core/tool/compiler.cxx`\\n**Main Class**: `ScCompiler` (extends `formula::FormulaCompiler`)\\n\\nThe `ScCompiler` class (lines 181-280+ in compiler.hxx) is responsible for:\\n- Parsing formula strings into tokens\\n- Converting formula text into bytecode (token array)\\n- Handling different formula grammars (ODS, XLSX, etc.)\\n- Maintaining character classification and convention handling\\n\\nKey responsibilities:\\n- Tokenization of formula expressions like `=SUM(A1:A10)`\\n- Creation of `ScTokenArray` objects containing the compiled formula\\n- Reference parsing and cell address conventions\\n\\n### 2. Formula Cell Type\\n\\n**Header File**: `sc/inc/formulacell.hxx`\\n**Implementation File**: `sc/source/core/data/formulacell.cxx`\\n**Main Class**: `ScFormulaCell`\\n\\nThe `ScFormulaCell` class (starting at line 150+ in formulacell.hxx) represents a spreadsheet cell containing a formula. Key features:\\n- **Constructors** (lines 197-225): Various constructors accepting formula strings, token arrays, or formula grammar\\n- **Interpret()** method (line 268): Triggers formula evaluation\\n- **SetDirty()** method (line 235): Marks cell for recalculation\\n- **Compile()** methods (lines 255-262): Parse formula string into tokens\\n- **InterpretTail()** method (line 184): Low-level interpretation logic\\n\\nThe `ScFormulaCell` holds:\\n- The compiled token array (`ScTokenArray`)\\n- The cell address (`ScAddress aPos`, line 190)\\n- Formula result and error state\\n- Recalculation flags\\n\\n### 3. Formula Bytecode Interpreter\\n\\n**Header File**: `sc/source/core/inc/interpre.hxx`\\n**Implementation Files**: Split across multiple files:\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr1.cxx` - Core interpreter\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr2.cxx` - Function implementations\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr3.cxx` - More functions\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr4.cxx` - Database/external functions\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr5.cxx` - Statistical functions\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr6.cxx` - Additional functions\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr7.cxx` - Matrix/array functions\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr8.cxx` - More specialized functions\\n\\n**Main Class**: `ScInterpreter` (starting at line 197 in interpre.hxx)\\n\\nThe `ScInterpreter` class implements bytecode execution:\\n- **Constructor** (line 1126): Initializes interpreter with cell, document, context, and token array\\n- **Interpret()** method (line 1138): Main entry point that executes the formula and returns result\\n- **Push/Pop operations**: Stack-based operations for formula evaluation\\n- **Function implementations**: Methods implementing each formula function (SUM, AVERAGE, etc.)\\n- **Type conversions**: Handles value conversions between types\\n\\nInternal state:\\n- `pArr`: Token array (line 244)\\n- `pStack`: Evaluation stack for operands (line 257)\\n- `nGlobalError`: Error code tracking (line 258)\\n- `sp`: Stack pointer (line 259)\\n- `pMyFormulaCell`: Reference to the cell being evaluated (line 253)\\n- `mrContext`: Interpreter context containing document reference (line 245)\\n\\n### 4. Recalculation Scheduling & Mode\\n\\n**Definition File**: `include/formula/tokenarray.hxx` (lines 59-69)\\n**Enum**: `ScRecalcMode`\\n\\nThe `ScRecalcMode` enum defines when formulas should be recalculated:\\n```cpp\\nenum class ScRecalcMode : sal_uInt8\\n{\\n    ALWAYS         = 0x01,  // exclusive, always recalculate\\n    ONLOAD_MUST    = 0x02,  // exclusive, always after load\\n    ONLOAD_ONCE    = 0x04,  // exclusive, once after load (import)\\n    ONLOAD_LENIENT = 0x08,  // exclusive, lenient after load\\n    NORMAL         = 0x10,  // exclusive, normal mode\\n    FORCED         = 0x20,  // combined, force even if not visible\\n    ONREFMOVE      = 0x40,  // combined, if reference moved\\n    EMask          = ...     // mask of exclusive bits\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Usage**: `ScFormulaCell::AddRecalcMode()` (line 388 in formulacell.hxx, implemented at line 2649 in formulacell.cxx)\\n- Marks formula cells for recalculation based on the mode\\n- Controls when cells are added to the recalculation queue\\n- Determines if cell results are volatile (always recalculate) or stable (only recalc when dirty)\\n\\n### Evaluation Chain Flow\\n\\n**Example: `=SUM(A1:A10)` enters a cell**\\n\\n1. **User enters formula** \u2192 `ScFormulaCell` constructor receives formula string\\n2. **Parsing Phase**: `ScCompiler::ParseFormula()` is called\\n   - Formula string is tokenized into operations and operands\\n   - Result: `ScTokenArray` with compiled tokens\\n   - Reference ranges (A1:A10) are identified and stored\\n   \\n3. **Storage**: `ScFormulaCell` stores the token array and registers listeners for referenced cells\\n\\n4. **Recalculation Decision**: `ScRecalcMode` determines if immediate recalc needed\\n   - NORMAL mode: Wait for dependency changes\\n   - ALWAYS mode: Recalculate every iteration\\n   - ONLOAD_MUST: Recalculate after file load\\n\\n5. **Evaluation Phase**: `ScFormulaCell::Interpret()` is called\\n   - Creates `ScInterpreter` instance with token array\\n   - Calls `ScInterpreter::Interpret()`\\n   - Interpreter walks token array, executing operations\\n   - Stack-based evaluation: pushes operands, executes functions\\n\\n6. **SUM Implementation**: In interpreter's SUM handler\\n   - Processes range A1:A10\\n   - Iterates cells, accumulates values\\n   - Returns sum result\\n\\n7. **Result Storage**: Result stored in `ScFormulaCell`\\n   - Sets result type and value\\n   - Updates format index if needed\\n   - Broadcasts change notification to dependent cells\\n\\n### Key Implementation Details\\n\\n- **Thread Safety**: `ScInterpreterContext` provides thread-safe access to document data\\n- **Error Handling**: `FormulaError` enum tracks calculation errors (division by zero, circular refs, etc.)\\n- **Matrix Support**: `ScMatrix` handles array formulas and matrix operations\\n- **External References**: Support for cross-document and cross-sheet references\\n- **Performance**: Multiple interpreter instances split across 8 implementation files for code organization\\n\"\n}\n",
